< Text>
What a gem to come across in this town in the middle of nowhere! Lots of craft brews on both tap and bottle, friendly and efficient service, great music playing on the stereo, and small and intimate atmosphere. If one is into the craft beer scene this is definitely the place to go in Redding. Highly recommended. No kitchen here though.<//Text>

<Text>The Alehouse is probably the best bar in Redding if you're a beer enthusiast.  They always have a ton of amazing brews on tap of basically every kind.  They have light ales, porters, a bunch of IPA's (my least favorite, but my friends who like IPA's Saturday they're good), and frequently at least a few sours.  The vibe is chill, the music is good, and the service is friendly.

It's a little spendy.  Parking isn't the best, but they share a lot with a chain sports bar, so you can easily park there.  That's it.  That's the extent of the negative portion of the review.

If you've got a few spare bills and want to try some excellent beers in a very relaxed atmosphere, go to the Alehouse.< /Text>< rate>
5</rate>

I want to like this place, in fact I want to love it - but I cant. Both times I have eaten here our server seems over worked, I don't see anyone helping her which creates a very slow experience. On my 3rd visit I couldn't wait  any longer as the family became too impatient to be seated. We were told 5-10 minutes and after 15 were told 5 more minutes, after that we left and went else where. There were two other parties in the resturant and a couple at the bar. Not busy to say the least. I give it 3 stars because the food is very, very good... when you finally get it that is. Otherwise it would be a 1 star experience. The folks seating us usually seem indifferent to guest mostly which should drop them to 1 star. But the ravioli is my favorite and the alfredo is great. I have other choices and must spend my money elsewhere though.< /text>

< review>
Just so so. Not great by any means. Not sure I understand the hype. It's Italian by name and by menu, but the quality screams Denny's. I paid $22 for some alfredo with (5) shrimp on it. And while the alfredo sauce definitely didn't come from a can, it quickly broke down into a puddle of grease at the bottom of my bowl. Also, the shrimp was previously frozen. The quality doesn't match the price one bit.

The service was very slow for a Thursday night. The restaurant was not at capacity and was well staffed. Still, our order came out after two other tables which larger groups that had ordered after us.

Maybe it was the food we ordered, maybe it was just us, maybe it was one of those so-called "off nights" for the restaurant, in any case we won't be back.</review>

< review>
An Italian-American surprise in a small town strip mall.   In town for some meetings and chose this place based off of its menu which indicated a few items were homemade.  I had the Sausage Miramonte (thick cut true Italian sausage, breaded eggplant... which was kind of soggy, fresh button mushrooms and an amazing fresh light red sauce); it came with a truly garlicy slice of bread, and a side salad with real anchovies.  So good. My server Katie was on top of it.   Pros+ good recipes, reasonable costs (most meals $13-18; early bird stuff about $10). Cons- Fake flower vases at table downgrade the restaurant, offer some fresh ground pepper on a true salad and pasta, vacant outdoor patio made it look like the place wasn't even open.<//review>

< review>
Absolutely horrible!

We arrived during lunch and were seated.  Unfortunately, we waited 15 minutes for someone to take our drink order.  During that time one of the waitresses and managers walked past us several times, while we heard them bicker over who would take care of us.

Ordered our meal, but watched it sit in the window for 10 minutes before it arrived luke warm.  A waitress refused to deliver it as she was rolling silver and it wasn't her table.  Apparently there is a personal greivance between staff.

The food quality was ridiculous.  One meal tasted like a Lean Cuisine, the other like Beef Stroganoff.  In short, horrible.

Wanted to inform someone that cared, but unfortunately the owners also perform a magic act, in which they vanished into thin-air...

Fortunately, this was my one and only visit.  Do yourself a favor.... Visit Stater Bros, buy a TV dinner and a beer for $5.  You'll be better off.< /review>
